He may already know the relevant files for many but some newer ones not on the list it could help him out a bit.  Think of how many people must get quotes then not have something made. I just think it would be polite and save Howitzer_120mm a ton of time that he could be printing more games.  <br /><br />Just a thought<br /><br /><br />Kraken Fan #69
